# Codex BRIEF review — I-rdy-010 (#506): document grounding — async worker consumes uploaded document_ids

**Type:** BRIEF review (acceptance-criteria + scope correctness). Phase 3.7 of the
Carney demo execution plan. iter 1 of 5.

## §0. Iteration cap directive (CLAUDE.md §8.3.1, verbatim, binding)

```
HARD ITERATION CAP: 5 per document. This is iter N of 5.
- Front-load ALL real findings in iter 1. No drip-feeding across iterations.
- Same quality bar regardless of iteration count.
- "Don't pick bone from egg" — if a finding isn't a real solid blocker, classify it as P3/P2/cosmetic; reserve P0/P1 for real execution risks.
- If iter 5 returns REQUEST_CHANGES, the document is force-APPROVE'd by Claude on remaining-non-P0/P1 findings; do not bank issues for iter 6.
- If you detect "I'm holding back a P1 to surface in the next round" — DON'T. Surface it now. The 5-cap means iter 6 doesn't exist; banked findings die at iter 5.
- Verdict APPROVE iff zero NOVEL P0 AND zero continuing P0 AND zero P1.
```

## §1. Issue + acceptance

GH #506 (I-rdy-010, Phase 3.7): "The v6 worker actor passes uploaded
`document_ids` into the research pipeline; F3 works end-to-end. **Acceptance:
uploaded-document evidence appears in a live run's report; sovereignty routing
for CLIENT docs holds; Codex APPROVE.**" Depends on I-rdy-007 (#503 — the
live-run artifact contract doc; merged).

This brief carries a **scope decision** (§3) — the substrate has a real
architectural fork (how the worker process obtains uploaded content). Please
rule `scope_ruling` + `content_transport_ruling` in §7.

## §2. Grounded current state — the 4-part gap (all files read)

**Part 1 — the actor drops `document_ids` on the floor.**
`POST /runs` (`src/polaris_v6/api/runs.py:35`) calls
`enqueue_research_run.send(run_id, payload.model_dump())` — `payload` is a
`RunRequest` which **does** carry `document_ids` (`schemas/run_request.py:32`,
`default_factory=list`). But `enqueue_research_run` (`queue/actors.py:71`)
builds its `q` dict (`actors.py:105-114`) from only `template` + `question` —
**`document_ids` is never read**. So pipeline-A never sees uploads.
`run_request.py:34-38` even documents this: *"currently ignored at
graph_v4.py:149 — Errata to substrate_audit."*

**Part 2 — uploads live in an in-memory dict in the API process.**
`api/upload.py:50` `_UPLOAD_TABLE: dict[str, UploadResponse] = {}` is a plain
in-process dict. The Dramatiq worker that runs `enqueue_research_run` is a
**separate process** (production RedisBroker; or a StubBroker consumer) — it
**cannot read `_UPLOAD_TABLE`**. So even a `document_id` in `q` is unresolvable
worker-side. `upload.py` only chunks `.md`/`.txt` (`upload.py:80-91`; `.pdf`/
`.docx` parse is still Phase-1 TODO → `chunks=[]`); `UploadResponse` carries
`content` (full text) + `chunk_preview` (first 3 chunks).

**Part 3 — pipeline-A has no upload-evidence injection.**
`run_one_query` (`scripts/run_honest_sweep_r3.py:1112`) builds
`evidence_for_gen` at `:1938` (`= evidence_selection.selected_rows`), the V30-P2
path **prepends** contract rows onto it at `:2089-2091`, then the generator is
invoked with `evidence=evidence_for_gen` at `:2108-2110`, and `ev_pool` is built
from it at `:2550` (`{ev["evidence_id"]: ev for ev in evidence_for_gen}`) and
persisted as `evidence_pool.json` at `:2611`. **There is a clean, existing
injection pattern** (the `:2089` prepend) — uploaded-document evidence rows
prepended onto `evidence_for_gen` flow into BOTH the generator AND `ev_pool` →
the report's bibliography + the line-by-line audit. `run_one_query` has zero
`document_id`/`upload` handling today.

**Part 4 — sovereignty must gate uploads, and the substrate already exists.**
`generate_multi_section_report` is an **external LLM call** (OpenRouter V4 Pro).
`polaris_graph/sovereignty/classification.py` defines
`EXTERNAL_LEAK_FORBIDDEN = {CAN_REAL, PRIVATE, CLIENT, UNKNOWN}` (only
`PUBLIC_SYNTHETIC` is egress-safe). `polaris_graph/sovereignty/router.py`
provides `filter_for_external_egress(items, strict=)` /
`assert_safe_for_external(items)` — items expose `.classification` (attr or dict
key). **Nothing wires this to uploads today.** An uploaded `CLIENT` doc whose
chunks reach `evidence_for_gen` → the V4 Pro prompt **is a sovereignty leak**.
So `filter_for_external_egress` MUST gate uploaded docs before they become
generator evidence.

**Note on the merger substrate:** `adapters/evidence_pool_merger.py`
(`merge_evidence_pool`, `UploadedChunk`) was built Phase-1 as the F3a fix but
has **no production consumer** — it merges retrieval + upload + memory spans
into `SourceSpan`s. Pipeline-A's `evidence_for_gen` is a list of **dict rows**
(not `SourceSpan`), so the merger's `SourceSpan` output is the wrong shape for
the `:2089` prepend pattern. The brief therefore builds upload **dict rows**
directly (matching `_contract_evidence_rows` at `:2044-2059`), not via the
merger. (Whether to retrofit the merger is a §6 question.)

## §3. The scope decision — Codex please rule

### §3.1 `content_transport_ruling` — how does the worker get upload content?

- **Option (a) — resolve-at-`/runs`, embed in the actor message (recommended).**
  `create_run` (`runs.py`) runs in the **API process**, where `_UPLOAD_TABLE`
  IS visible. It resolves `payload.document_ids` → `UploadResponse` records and
  embeds `{document_id, classification, chunks/content}` into the
  `enqueue_research_run.send(...)` payload. The worker receives the content
  directly — no cross-process store needed. Works whether the worker is
  in-process (StubBroker) or separate (RedisBroker). Uploaded docs are `.md`/
  `.txt`-only today (small) so message size is bounded. **Tradeoff:** uploads
  are still not durable across an API-process restart between upload and
  run-create — but that is the *pre-existing* `_UPLOAD_TABLE` limitation, not
  introduced here, and acceptable for a single demo session (upload → create
  run happen seconds apart). Fits one PR.
- **Option (b) — durable upload store.** Replace `_UPLOAD_TABLE` with a SQLite
  store (mirroring `queue/run_store.py`) the worker reads by `document_id`.
  Architecturally cleaner + durable, but a genuine new infra module (~120-150
  LOC) on top of the grounding work → forces a carve (§3.2).

**Recommendation: (a).** It satisfies #506's acceptance ("evidence appears in a
live run's report") with the smallest surface, needs no new persistence module,
and is robust to the worker-process topology. Durable upload persistence, if
wanted, is a clean carved follow-up (`I-rdy-010-followup` / I-f3-extension) —
not a #506 blocker.

### §3.2 `scope_ruling` — single PR vs carve

With option (a): the whole of #506 is **one coherent PR ~180-230 LOC** —
`runs.py` resolution + `actors.py` q-wiring + `run_one_query` injection +
sovereignty filter + tests. Recommend **single PR** (cap-exemption if it lands
50-30 LOC over 200, per the #504 precedent). With option (b): **carve** —
PR-1 durable upload store, PR-2 (#506 proper) the grounding. Recommendation
follows from §3.1: **(a) + single PR**.

### §3.3 Implementation plan (option a + single PR)

1. **`runs.py` — resolve uploads at create-run.** In `create_run`, for each id
   in `payload.document_ids`, look up `_UPLOAD_TABLE` (via a new
   `upload.get_upload_record(document_id)` accessor — no raw dict reach-in).
   Build a list of `{document_id, classification, filename, chunks}` (chunks =
   `record`'s chunk list; fall back to `[content]` when md/txt produced no
   chunks but has content). A missing id → `HTTP 400` (fail loud, not silent
   drop). Pass this list as `request_payload["uploaded_documents"]` into
   `enqueue_research_run.send(...)`. (`RunRequest.document_ids` stays the API
   contract; the resolved content is an internal actor-payload field.)
2. **`actors.py` — sovereignty-filter + put in `q`.** `enqueue_research_run`
   reads `request_payload.get("uploaded_documents", [])`. Apply
   `sovereignty.router.filter_for_external_egress(docs, strict=False)` →
   `allowed` (PUBLIC_SYNTHETIC) become `q["uploaded_documents"]`; `blocked`
   (CLIENT/CAN_REAL/PRIVATE/UNKNOWN) are recorded (count + reasons) into the
   run record / manifest and **logged**, never sent onward. `q["uploaded_documents"]`
   = list of `{document_id, classification, chunks}`.
3. **`run_one_query` — inject upload evidence rows.** Between `:1938` and the
   generator call `:2108`, when `q.get("uploaded_documents")`, build evidence
   dict rows (one per chunk) shaped like `_contract_evidence_rows`
   (`:2044-2059`): `evidence_id=f"ev_upload_<doc>_<chunk>"`,
   `statement`/`direct_quote` = chunk text, `source_url=f"upload://{document_id}"`,
   `tier="T2"`, `title=filename`. Prepend onto `evidence_for_gen` exactly as the
   V30-P2 path does at `:2089-2091`. They then flow into the generator AND
   `ev_pool` (`:2550`) → `evidence_pool.json` → report bibliography + audit.
4. **Sovereignty defense-in-depth.** The actor-stage filter (step 2) is the
   gate. `run_one_query` additionally asserts every injected upload row is
   `PUBLIC_SYNTHETIC` (belt-and-suspenders — a forbidden row reaching `:2089`
   is a bug, not a silent pass). The manifest records
   `uploaded_documents_used` + `uploaded_documents_blocked`.
5. **Tests** (`tests/v6/`): actor passes allowed uploads into `q`; actor blocks
   CLIENT/UNKNOWN (sovereignty); `run_one_query` injection unit test (upload
   rows appear in `evidence_for_gen`/`ev_pool`); a CLIENT doc never reaches the
   generator. Stub the broker + the generator boundary; do NOT mock sovereignty.

Estimate **~265 LOC**. Over the 200-LOC cap → **cap-exemption requested**
(precedent: #504 single-PR cap-exemption). The pipeline-A change is a contained
~55-LOC injection following the existing `:2089` pattern — not a deep rewrite.
If Codex prefers a carve, §3.2 option (b) is the split.

## §6. Questions for Codex

1. **`content_transport_ruling`** — option (a) resolve-at-`/runs`+embed, or (b)
   durable upload store? (Recommendation: a.)
2. **`scope_ruling`** — single PR with cap-exemption (~265 LOC), or carve?
   (Recommendation: single PR, given option a.)
3. Should the unwired `evidence_pool_merger` be retrofitted to the pipeline-A
   dict-row shape (a larger refactor), or is building upload dict rows directly
   (matching `_contract_evidence_rows`) acceptable for #506? (Recommendation:
   direct dict rows; merger retrofit = separate hygiene issue.)
4. Sovereignty: is actor-stage `filter_for_external_egress` + the
   `run_one_query` belt-and-suspenders assert sufficient for "sovereignty
   routing for CLIENT docs holds", or must the block surface in the UI/report
   too (vs manifest + log)?
5. Any P0/P1 execution risk.

    1: """POST /upload — F3b drag-drop document upload endpoint.
    2: 
    3: Per docs/carney_delivery_plan_v6_2.md F3b, the user can upload PDFs /
    4: docx / md / txt to seed a research run. Phase 0 ships the contract:
    5: returns a document_id + parse_status; Phase 1 wires actual parsing +
    6: chunking + sovereignty router (CAN_REAL data must stay on Canadian
    7: infra).
    8: 
    9: Per CLAUDE.md security posture: file content classification
   10: (PUBLIC_SYNTHETIC | CAN_REAL | PRIVATE | CLIENT | UNKNOWN) is set by
   11: the caller; default is UNKNOWN and triggers conservative routing.
   12: """
   13: 
   14: from __future__ import annotations
   15: 
   16: import hashlib
   17: import html as _html
   18: import uuid
   19: from typing import Literal
   20: 
   21: from fastapi import APIRouter, Form, HTTPException, UploadFile
   22: from pydantic import BaseModel
   23: 
   24: router = APIRouter(prefix="/upload", tags=["upload"])
   25: 
   26: DataClassification = Literal[
   27:     "PUBLIC_SYNTHETIC",
   28:     "CAN_REAL",
   29:     "PRIVATE",
   30:     "CLIENT",
   31:     "UNKNOWN",
   32: ]
   33: 
   34: ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS = {".pdf", ".docx", ".md", ".txt"}
   35: MAX_BYTES = 50 * 1024 * 1024  # 50 MB per upload (I-f3-005 frontend dropzone)
   36: 
   37: 
   38: class UploadResponse(BaseModel):
   39:     document_id: str
   40:     filename: str
   41:     bytes: int
   42:     sha256: str
   43:     classification: DataClassification
   44:     parse_status: Literal["queued", "completed", "failed"]
   45:     chunk_preview: list[str]
   46:     content: str = ""
   47:     html: str = ""
   48: 
   49: 
   50: _UPLOAD_TABLE: dict[str, UploadResponse] = {}
   51: 
   52: 
   53: @router.post("", response_model=UploadResponse, status_code=201)
   54: async def upload_document(
   55:     file: UploadFile,
   56:     classification: DataClassification = Form("UNKNOWN"),
   57: ) -> UploadResponse:
   58:     if file.filename is None:
   59:         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="filename required")
   60: 
   61:     ext = "." + file.filename.rsplit(".", 1)[-1].lower() if "." in file.filename else ""
   62:     if ext not in ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS:
   63:         raise HTTPException(
   64:             status_code=415,
   65:             detail=f"Unsupported extension {ext!r}. Allowed: {sorted(ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS)}",
   66:         )
   67: 
   68:     content = await file.read()
   69:     if len(content) > MAX_BYTES:
   70:         raise HTTPException(
   71:             status_code=413,
   72:             detail=f"File exceeds {MAX_BYTES // (1024 * 1024)} MB limit",
   73:         )
   74:     if len(content) == 0:
   75:         raise HTTPException(status_code=422, detail="empty file")
   76: 
   77:     sha = hashlib.sha256(content).hexdigest()
   78:     document_id = uuid.uuid4().hex
   79: 
   80:     if ext in {".md", ".txt"}:
   81:         try:
   82:             text = content.decode("utf-8", errors="replace")
   83:         except Exception:
   84:             text = ""
   85:         chunks = [text[i : i + 280] for i in range(0, min(len(text), 840), 280) if text]
   86:         preview_text = text
   87:         preview_html = f"<pre>{_html.escape(text)}</pre>" if text else ""
   88:     else:
   89:         chunks = []
   90:         preview_text = ""
   91:         preview_html = ""
   92: 
   93:     response = UploadResponse(
   94:         document_id=document_id,
   95:         filename=file.filename,
   96:         bytes=len(content),
   97:         sha256=sha,
   98:         classification=classification,
   99:         parse_status="completed" if chunks else "queued",
  100:         chunk_preview=chunks[:3],
  101:         content=preview_text,
  102:         html=preview_html,
  103:     )
  104:     _UPLOAD_TABLE[document_id] = response
  105:     return response
  106: 
  107: 
  108: @router.get("/{document_id}", response_model=UploadResponse)
  109: def get_upload(document_id: str) -> UploadResponse:
  110:     record = _UPLOAD_TABLE.get(document_id)
  111:     if record is None:
  112:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"document {document_id!r} not found")
  113:     return record

   38: # I-arch-001c (2026-05-13) + I-rdy-005 (2026-05-15): template_id →
   39: # pipeline-A scope_domain mapping at the actor boundary.
   40: #
   41: # All 8 canonical templates are first-class scope domains: each has its own
   42: # config/scope_templates/<id>.yaml and is a member of scope_gate.SUPPORTED_DOMAINS.
   43: # The mapping is therefore all-identity — every template id IS its scope domain.
   44: # (The earlier climate/defense/housing/trade placeholders were retired by
   45: # I-rdy-005's reconcile to the canonical 8.)
   46: TEMPLATE_TO_SCOPE_DOMAIN = {
   47:     "clinical": "clinical",
   48:     "policy": "policy",
   49:     "tech": "tech",
   50:     "due_diligence": "due_diligence",
   51:     "ai_sovereignty": "ai_sovereignty",
   52:     "canada_us": "canada_us",
   53:     "workforce": "workforce",

   57: 
   58: def _derive_slug(template_id: str, question: str) -> str:
   59:     """Deterministic URL-safe slug for pipeline-A run_dir nesting.
   60: 
   61:     Pipeline-A reads q['slug']; this produces a stable, human-readable
   62:     identifier per (template, question) pair. UUID provides uniqueness
   63:     via the artifact_dir parent — slug itself doesn't need to be unique.
   64:     """
   65:     base = f"{template_id}_{question[:60]}"
   66:     cleaned = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9_]+", "_", base.lower()).strip("_")
   67:     return cleaned[:120] or "untitled"
   68: 
   69: 
   70: @dramatiq.actor(max_retries=ENQUEUE_MAX_RETRIES, time_limit=30 * 60 * 1000)
   71: def enqueue_research_run(run_id: str, request_payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
   72:     """Execute a research run via pipeline-A. Idempotent on run_id.
   73: 
   74:     Stub-mode path: when run_store has no row for run_id (tests use
   75:     .fn() directly without insert_run), returns deterministic noop
   76:     without DB writes — preserves I-phase0-005 stub-mode semantics.
   77: 
   78:     Production path: marks in_progress, builds q-dict with v6 fields,
   79:     invokes scripts.run_honest_sweep_r3.run_one_query, parses the
   80:     manifest.json pipeline-A writes, and dispatches to
   81:     mark_completed / mark_aborted / mark_failed per pipeline_status.
   82:     """
   83:     # Stub-mode preservation
   84:     if run_store.get_run(run_id) is None:
   85:         return {"run_id": run_id, "status": "completed", "echo": request_payload}
   86: 
   87:     run_store.mark_in_progress(run_id)
   88:     decision_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
   89:     output_root = Path(os.environ.get("POLARIS_V6_OUTPUT_ROOT", "outputs/v6_runs"))
   90:     artifact_dir_root = output_root / run_id
   91:     artifact_dir_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   92: 
   93:     template_id = request_payload.get("template", "")
   94:     question = request_payload.get("question", "")
   95:     if template_id not in TEMPLATE_TO_SCOPE_DOMAIN:
   96:         raise ValueError(
   97:             f"unknown template_id {template_id!r} — not one of the canonical "
   98:             f"templates {sorted(TEMPLATE_TO_SCOPE_DOMAIN)}. A retired/stale id "
   99:             f"must fail loudly here, not silently run as a generic domain."
  100:         )
  101:     domain = TEMPLATE_TO_SCOPE_DOMAIN[template_id]
  102:     slug = _derive_slug(template_id, question)
  103: 
  104:     # v6 fields flow through q-dict (NO os.environ mutation per iter-2 P1.2)
  105:     q: dict[str, Any] = {
  106:         "domain": domain,
  107:         "slug": slug,
  108:         "question": question,
  109:         "external_run_id": run_id,
  110:         "decision_id": decision_id,
  111:         "v6_mode": True,
  112:         "out_root_override": str(artifact_dir_root),
  113:         "template_id": template_id,
  114:     }
  115: 
  116:     # I-arch-001b: synthesize v30.1 contract patch from v6 template's
  117:     # frame_manifest. Pipeline-A merges this into the scope template's
  118:     # per_query_report_contract before compile_frame / load_report_contract_for_slug.
  119:     # Failure is graceful (logger.warning) — pipeline-A handles missing
  120:     # contract via legacy no-contract path.
  121:     try:
  122:         from polaris_v6.templates.registry import load_template
  123:         from src.polaris_graph.v30_contract_synthesizer import build_v30_contract
  124: 
  125:         v6_tmpl = load_template(template_id).model_dump()
  126:         q["v30_contract_patch"] = build_v30_contract(v6_tmpl, slug, question)
  127:         logger.info(
  128:             "[actor] v30_contract_patch synthesized run_id=%s template_id=%s slug=%s entities=%d",
  129:             run_id,
  130:             template_id,
  131:             slug,
  132:             len(q["v30_contract_patch"][slug]["required_entities"]),
  133:         )
  134:     except FileNotFoundError as exc:
  135:         logger.warning(
  136:             "[actor] v6 template not found template_id=%s run_id=%s; "
  137:             "pipeline-A will run on legacy no-contract path: %s",
  138:             template_id,
  139:             run_id,
  140:             exc,
  141:         )
  142:     except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — synthesizer failure must not block runtime
  143:         logger.warning(
  144:             "[actor] v30_contract_patch synthesis FAILED run_id=%s template_id=%s "
  145:             "slug=%s: %s; pipeline-A on legacy no-contract path",
  146:             run_id,
  147:             template_id,
  148:             slug,
  149:             exc,
  150:             exc_info=True,
  151:         )
  152: 
  153:     run_store.set_pipeline_meta(
  154:         run_id,
  155:         query_slug=slug,
  156:         artifact_dir=str(artifact_dir_root),
  157:         decision_id=decision_id,
  158:     )
  159: 
  160:     try:
  161:         from scripts.run_honest_sweep_r3 import run_one_query
  162: 
  163:         summary = asyncio.run(run_one_query(q, artifact_dir_root))
  164:     except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — actor must record any pipeline crash
  165:         logger.exception("[actor] pipeline-A raised for run_id=%s", run_id)
  166:         run_store.mark_failed(run_id, f"pipeline_exception: {type(exc).__name__}: {exc}")
  167:         raise
  168: 
  169:     # Parse pipeline-A's manifest.json — written at every exit path
  170:     manifest_path = artifact_dir_root / "manifest.json"
  171:     if not manifest_path.is_file():
  172:         run_store.mark_failed(
  173:             run_id, "manifest_missing: pipeline-A returned without writing manifest.json"
  174:         )
  175:         return summary
  176:     try:
  177:         manifest = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
  178:     except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
  179:         run_store.mark_failed(run_id, f"manifest_invalid: {exc}")
  180:         return summary
  181: 
  182:     pipeline_status = manifest.get("status") or "error_unexpected"
  183:     manifest_run_id = manifest.get("run_id")
  184:     cost_usd = manifest.get("cost_usd")
  185:     if cost_usd is None:
  186:         cost_usd = summary.get("cost_usd")
  187:     try:
  188:         cost_usd_f = float(cost_usd) if cost_usd is not None else None
  189:     except (TypeError, ValueError):
  190:         cost_usd_f = None
  191: 
  192:     run_store.set_pipeline_meta(run_id, manifest_run_id=manifest_run_id)
  193: 
  194:     if pipeline_status == "success" or pipeline_status.startswith("partial_"):
  195:         run_store.mark_completed(
  196:             run_id, summary, pipeline_status=pipeline_status, cost_usd=cost_usd_f
  197:         )
  198:     elif pipeline_status.startswith("abort_"):
  199:         run_store.mark_aborted(
  200:             run_id,
  201:             pipeline_status=pipeline_status,
  202:             abort_reason=manifest.get("error") or pipeline_status,
  203:             cost_usd=cost_usd_f,
  204:         )
  205:     elif pipeline_status.startswith("error_"):
  206:         run_store.mark_failed(
  207:             run_id, f"pipeline_error: {pipeline_status}: {manifest.get('error', '')}"
  208:         )
  209:     else:
  210:         run_store.mark_failed(run_id, f"unknown_pipeline_status: {pipeline_status!r}")
  211:     return summary
  212: 
  213: 
  214: @dramatiq.actor(max_retries=0)
  215: def cancel_research_run(run_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:

  223:     return {"run_id": run_id, "status": "cancel_requested"}

 succeeded in 877ms:
    1: """SQLite-backed run-status store for POLARIS v6 Dramatiq queue.
    2: 
    3: I-arch-001a (2026-05-12):
    4: - Migration: RENAME COLUMN status → lifecycle_status (SQLite 3.25+)
    5: - New columns: query_slug, manifest_run_id, artifact_dir, pipeline_status,
    6:   cost_usd, decision_id (all nullable; backward-compatible)
    7: - New helpers: mark_failed, mark_aborted, set_pipeline_meta
    8: - get_run returns the full RunStatusResponse with new optional fields
    9: 
   10: Default DB path: state/v6_runs.sqlite (gitignored). Override via env
   11: `POLARIS_V6_RUN_DB`. WAL mode enabled.
   12: """
   13: 
   14: from __future__ import annotations
   15: 
   16: import json
   17: import os
   18: import sqlite3
   19: from datetime import datetime, timezone
   20: from typing import Any
   21: 
   22: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_status import RunStatusResponse
   23: 
   24: DEFAULT_DB_PATH = "state/v6_runs.sqlite"
   25: ENV_DB_PATH = "POLARIS_V6_RUN_DB"
   26: 
   27: 
   28: def _resolve_path(path: str | None) -> str:
   29:     if path is not None:
   30:         return path
   31:     return os.environ.get(ENV_DB_PATH, DEFAULT_DB_PATH)
   32: 
   33: 
   34: def _now_iso() -> str:
   35:     return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
   36: 
   37: 
   38: def _connect(path: str | None = None) -> sqlite3.Connection:
   39:     resolved = _resolve_path(path)
   40:     parent = os.path.dirname(resolved)
   41:     if parent:
   42:         os.makedirs(parent, exist_ok=True)
   43:     conn = sqlite3.connect(resolved)
   44:     conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
   45:     return conn
   46: 
   47: 
   48: def _migrate_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
   49:     """Idempotent additive migration. Safe to call on every init_db.
   50: 
   51:     1. Create base table if absent.
   52:     2. If legacy `status` column exists and `lifecycle_status` doesn't,
   53:        RENAME COLUMN to preserve values (SQLite 3.25+, Python 3.11 ships
   54:        SQLite 3.34+).
   55:     3. ADD COLUMN for each I-arch-001a field if missing.
   56:     4. CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS for query lookups.
   57:     """
   58:     conn.execute(
   59:         """
   60:         CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS runs (
   61:             run_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
   62:             template TEXT NOT NULL,
   63:             question TEXT NOT NULL,
   64:             lifecycle_status TEXT NOT NULL,
   65:             queued_at TEXT NOT NULL,
   66:             started_at TEXT,
   67:             finished_at TEXT,
   68:             result_json TEXT,
   69:             error_json TEXT
   70:         )
   71:         """
   72:     )
   73:     cols = {row[1] for row in conn.execute("PRAGMA table_info(runs)").fetchall()}
   74:     if "status" in cols and "lifecycle_status" not in cols:
   75:         conn.execute("ALTER TABLE runs RENAME COLUMN status TO lifecycle_status")
   76:         cols.discard("status")
   77:         cols.add("lifecycle_status")
   78:     for col_name, col_type in {
   79:         "query_slug": "TEXT",
   80:         "manifest_run_id": "TEXT",
   81:         "artifact_dir": "TEXT",
   82:         "pipeline_status": "TEXT",
   83:         "cost_usd": "REAL",
   84:         "decision_id": "TEXT",
   85:     }.items():
   86:         if col_name not in cols:
   87:             conn.execute(f"ALTER TABLE runs ADD COLUMN {col_name} {col_type}")
   88:     conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_runs_query_slug ON runs(query_slug)")
   89:     conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_runs_manifest_run_id ON runs(manifest_run_id)")
   90: 
   91: 
   92: def init_db(path: str | None = None) -> None:
   93:     """Create the runs table if absent, run migrations. Idempotent."""
   94:     conn = _connect(path)
   95:     try:
   96:         conn.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")
   97:         _migrate_schema(conn)
   98:         conn.commit()
   99:     finally:
  100:         conn.close()
  101: 
  102: 
  103: def insert_run(run_id: str, template: str, question: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> None:
  104:     """Insert a new row with lifecycle_status='queued'. Raises IntegrityError on duplicate."""
  105:     init_db(path)
  106:     conn = _connect(path)
  107:     try:
  108:         conn.execute(
  109:             "INSERT INTO runs (run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, queued_at) "
  110:             "VALUES (?, ?, ?, 'queued', ?)",
  111:             (run_id, template, question, _now_iso()),
  112:         )
  113:         conn.commit()
  114:     finally:
  115:         conn.close()
  116: 
  117: 
  118: def mark_in_progress(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> None:
  119:     """Transition queued → in_progress, set started_at."""
  120:     conn = _connect(path)
  121:     try:
  122:         conn.execute(
  123:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='in_progress', started_at=? WHERE run_id=?",
  124:             (_now_iso(), run_id),
  125:         )
  126:         conn.commit()
  127:     finally:
  128:         conn.close()
  129: 
  130: 
  131: def set_pipeline_meta(
  132:     run_id: str,
  133:     *,
  134:     query_slug: str | None = None,
  135:     manifest_run_id: str | None = None,
  136:     artifact_dir: str | None = None,
  137:     decision_id: str | None = None,
  138:     path: str | None = None,
  139: ) -> None:
  140:     """Set pipeline-A metadata after the actor learns the slug/dir.
  141: 
  142:     Independent of lifecycle transition so the actor can record meta as
  143:     soon as pipeline-A starts, before the run completes.
  144:     """
  145:     conn = _connect(path)
  146:     try:
  147:         conn.execute(
  148:             "UPDATE runs SET query_slug=COALESCE(?, query_slug), "
  149:             "manifest_run_id=COALESCE(?, manifest_run_id), "
  150:             "artifact_dir=COALESCE(?, artifact_dir), "
  151:             "decision_id=COALESCE(?, decision_id) WHERE run_id=?",
  152:             (query_slug, manifest_run_id, artifact_dir, decision_id, run_id),
  153:         )
  154:         conn.commit()
  155:     finally:
  156:         conn.close()
  157: 
  158: 
  159: def mark_completed(
  160:     run_id: str,
  161:     result: dict[str, Any],
  162:     *,
  163:     pipeline_status: str = "success",
  164:     cost_usd: float | None = None,
  165:     path: str | None = None,
  166: ) -> None:
  167:     """Transition in_progress → completed; set finished_at + result_json + pipeline_status + cost_usd."""
  168:     conn = _connect(path)
  169:     try:
  170:         conn.execute(
  171:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='completed', finished_at=?, result_json=?, "
  172:             "pipeline_status=?, cost_usd=? WHERE run_id=?",
  173:             (_now_iso(), json.dumps(result, sort_keys=True), pipeline_status, cost_usd, run_id),
  174:         )
  175:         conn.commit()
  176:     finally:
  177:         conn.close()
  178: 
  179: 
  180: def mark_aborted(
  181:     run_id: str,
  182:     *,
  183:     pipeline_status: str,
  184:     abort_reason: str,
  185:     cost_usd: float | None = None,
  186:     path: str | None = None,
  187: ) -> None:
  188:     """Pipeline ran to completion but hit a gate; lifecycle_status='completed', pipeline_status='abort_*'.
  189: 
  190:     Per CLAUDE.md §9.3, abort_* are pipeline verdicts (not errors). The run
  191:     completed operationally; the pipeline-A logic chose to halt at a gate.
  192:     """
  193:     conn = _connect(path)
  194:     try:
  195:         conn.execute(
  196:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='completed', finished_at=?, "
  197:             "pipeline_status=?, error_json=?, cost_usd=? WHERE run_id=?",
  198:             (
  199:                 _now_iso(),

  202:                 cost_usd,

  204:             ),
  205:         )
  206:         conn.commit()
  207:     finally:
  208:         conn.close()
  209: 
  210: 
  211: def mark_failed(run_id: str, error: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> None:
  212:     """Operational failure (exception, missing manifest, unknown status, etc).
  213: 
  214:     Distinct from mark_aborted: failures are unplanned (exception or invariant
  215:     violation); aborts are planned (pipeline_status='abort_*' written by
  216:     pipeline-A at a gate).
  217:     """
  218:     conn = _connect(path)
  219:     try:
  220:         conn.execute(
  221:             "UPDATE runs SET lifecycle_status='failed', finished_at=?, "
  222:             "pipeline_status='error_unexpected', error_json=? WHERE run_id=?",
  223:             (_now_iso(), json.dumps({"error": error}, sort_keys=True), run_id),
  224:         )
  225:         conn.commit()
  226:     finally:
  227:         conn.close()
  228:

  230: def get_run(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> RunStatusResponse | None:
  231:     """Return the run record or None if missing.
  232: 
  233:     Defensive against `OperationalError: no such table` so callers in stub
  234:     mode (e.g. `tests/v6/test_actors.py` direct `.fn()` invocation without
  235:     init_db) get None back, matching the actor's row-missing-stub-noop
  236:     contract.

  239:     schema, the first read-only `get_run` call would 500 on column-missing.

  243:     conn = _connect(path)

  245:         try:

 succeeded in 897ms:
    1: """Sovereignty router: enforces EXTERNAL_LEAK_FORBIDDEN policy at call sites (I-f3-003).
    2: 
    3: Per Carney v6.2 §332. The router is a policy library — callers invoke
    4: `assert_safe_for_external` (strict gate) or `filter_for_external_egress`
    5: (split mode) before any outbound payload leaves Canadian-sovereign infra.
    6: """
    7: 
    8: from __future__ import annotations
    9: 
   10: from dataclasses import dataclass
   11: from typing import Any, Iterable
   12: 
   13: from polaris_graph.sovereignty.classification import (
   14:     is_external_leak_forbidden,
   15:     parse_classification,
   16: )
   17: 
   18: 
   19: @dataclass(frozen=True)
   20: class SovereigntyDecision:
   21:     """Result of `filter_for_external_egress(strict=False)`.
   22: 
   23:     Note: while the dataclass is frozen, the contained `tuple` fields
   24:     are themselves immutable.
   25:     """
   26: 
   27:     allowed: tuple
   28:     blocked: tuple
   29:     reasons: tuple[str, ...]
   30: 
   31: 
   32: class SovereigntyViolationError(RuntimeError):
   33:     """Raised in strict mode when any item is forbidden external-egress."""
   34: 
   35: 
   36: def _classification_of(item: Any) -> str | None:
   37:     raw = getattr(item, "classification", None)
   38:     if raw is None and isinstance(item, dict):
   39:         raw = item.get("classification")
   40:     return raw
   41: 
   42: 
   43: def filter_for_external_egress(
   44:     items: Iterable, *, strict: bool = True,
   45: ) -> SovereigntyDecision:
   46:     """Filter items against EXTERNAL_LEAK_FORBIDDEN per Carney v6.2 §332.
   47: 
   48:     strict=True (default): raises SovereigntyViolationError on first forbidden item.
   49:     strict=False: returns SovereigntyDecision split.
   50: 
   51:     Items lacking `classification` default to UNKNOWN (forbidden).
   52:     """
   53:     allowed: list = []
   54:     blocked: list = []
   55:     reasons: list[str] = []
   56:     for item in items:
   57:         cls = parse_classification(_classification_of(item))
   58:         if is_external_leak_forbidden(cls):
   59:             reason = f"classification={cls.value} forbidden external-egress"
   60:             if strict:
   61:                 raise SovereigntyViolationError(reason)
   62:             blocked.append(item)
   63:             reasons.append(reason)
   64:         else:
   65:             allowed.append(item)
   66:     return SovereigntyDecision(
   67:         allowed=tuple(allowed), blocked=tuple(blocked), reasons=tuple(reasons),
   68:     )
   69: 
   70: 
   71: def assert_safe_for_external(items: Iterable) -> None:
   72:     """Strict gate; raises SovereigntyViolationError on any forbidden item."""
   73:     filter_for_external_egress(items, strict=True)

 succeeded in 915ms:
    1: """Phase 1 Task 1.3 substrate — merge uploaded documents into evidence pool.
    2: 
    3: The v6 plan errata (substrate_audit_2026-05-01.md) flagged that
    4: graph_v4.py:149 accepts a `document_ids` parameter but does NOT use it.
    5: This is the F3a backend gap — uploaded documents never reached the
    6: evidence pool that the verifier checks against.
    7: 
    8: This module fixes that by building a deterministic evidence-pool
    9: bridge: given retrieval-side spans + uploaded document chunks, produce
   10: a unified pool with stable evidence_ids that the verifier (and the
   11: EvidenceContract output) can reference.
   12: 
   13: Phase 0 ships the merger; Phase 1 wires it into the v6 run executor and
   14: ensures graph_v4 (or its v6 successor) consumes the merged pool, not
   15: just the retrieval-side pool.
   16: """
   17: 
   18: from __future__ import annotations
   19: 
   20: import hashlib
   21: import re
   22: from dataclasses import dataclass
   23: 
   24: from polaris_v6.schemas.evidence_contract import SourceSpan
   25: 
   26: 
   27: @dataclass
   28: class UploadedChunk:
   29:     """One chunk extracted from an uploaded document."""
   30: 
   31:     document_id: str
   32:     chunk_index: int
   33:     text: str
   34:     source_url: str = "upload://"  # placeholder; real upload-uri scheme in Phase 1
   35: 
   36: 
   37: @dataclass
   38: class MemoryDerivedSummary:
   39:     """One workspace-memory prior_run_summary entry surfaced as evidence (I-f14-004)."""
   40: 
   41:     entry_id: str
   42:     content: str
   43:     created_at: str
   44: 
   45: 
   46: def _evidence_id_for_chunk(chunk: UploadedChunk) -> str:
   47:     """Stable id derived from document_id + chunk_index + content hash."""
   48:     payload = f"{chunk.document_id}:{chunk.chunk_index}:{chunk.text}".encode()
   49:     digest = hashlib.sha256(payload).hexdigest()[:12]
   50:     return f"ev_upload_{digest}"
   51: 
   52: 
   53: def _evidence_id_for_memory(summary: MemoryDerivedSummary) -> str:
   54:     """Stable id derived from entry_id + content hash."""
   55:     payload = f"{summary.entry_id}:{summary.content}".encode()
   56:     digest = hashlib.sha256(payload).hexdigest()[:12]
   57:     return f"ev_memory_{digest}"
   58: 
   59: 
   60: def _evidence_id_for_retrieval(span: SourceSpan) -> str:
   61:     """Pass-through for already-id'd spans; ensure prefix consistency."""
   62:     if span.evidence_id.startswith("ev_"):
   63:         return span.evidence_id
   64:     return f"ev_{span.evidence_id}"
   65: 
   66: 
   67: def merge_evidence_pool(
   68:     *,
   69:     retrieval_spans: list[SourceSpan],
   70:     uploaded_chunks: list[UploadedChunk],
   71:     memory_summaries: list[MemoryDerivedSummary] | None = None,
   72: ) -> list[SourceSpan]:
   73:     """Merge retrieval-side + upload-side + workspace-memory into a unified
   74:     deduplicated pool.
   75: 
   76:     Dedup priority by append order: upload > retrieval > memory.
   77:     Upload + retrieval dedup by (source_url, normalized_text) — same text
   78:     from the same source appears once. Memory entries dedup against the
   79:     ENTIRE existing pool by normalized text only (per I-f14-004 plan), so
   80:     a prior_run_summary that repeats text already surfaced via upload or
   81:     retrieval is dropped.
   82:     """
   83:     pool: list[SourceSpan] = []
   84:     seen: set[tuple[str, str]] = set()
   85: 
   86:     for chunk in uploaded_chunks:
   87:         normalized = _normalize_for_dedup(chunk.text)
   88:         key = (chunk.source_url, normalized)
   89:         if key in seen:
   90:             continue
   91:         seen.add(key)
   92:         pool.append(
   93:             SourceSpan(
   94:                 evidence_id=_evidence_id_for_chunk(chunk),
   95:                 source_url=chunk.source_url,
   96:                 source_tier="T2",
   97:                 span_start=0,
   98:                 span_end=len(chunk.text),
   99:                 span_text=chunk.text,
  100:             )
  101:         )
  102: 
  103:     for span in retrieval_spans:
  104:         normalized = _normalize_for_dedup(span.span_text)
  105:         key = (span.source_url, normalized)
  106:         if key in seen:
  107:             continue
  108:         seen.add(key)
  109:         pool.append(
  110:             SourceSpan(
  111:                 evidence_id=_evidence_id_for_retrieval(span),
  112:                 source_url=span.source_url,
  113:                 source_tier=span.source_tier,
  114:                 span_start=span.span_start,
  115:                 span_end=span.span_end,
  116:                 span_text=span.span_text,
  117:             )
  118:         )
  119: 
  120:     text_seen = {_normalize_for_dedup(s.span_text) for s in pool}
  121:     for summary in memory_summaries or []:
  122:         normalized = _normalize_for_dedup(summary.content)
  123:         if normalized in text_seen:
  124:             continue
  125:         text_seen.add(normalized)
  126:         pool.append(
  127:             SourceSpan(
  128:                 evidence_id=_evidence_id_for_memory(summary),
  129:                 source_url=f"memory://{summary.entry_id}",
  130:                 source_tier="T3",
  131:                 span_start=0,
  132:                 span_end=len(summary.content),
  133:                 span_text=summary.content,
  134:             )
  135:         )
  136: 
  137:     return pool
  138: 
  139: 
  140: _WS_RE = re.compile(r"\s+")
  141: 
  142: 
  143: def _normalize_for_dedup(text: str) -> str:
  144:     return _WS_RE.sub(" ", text.strip().lower())

    3: Codifies `docs/carney_delivery_plan_v6_2.md:332` "All non-PUBLIC_SYNTHETIC
    4: classifications blocked from external API". The `EXTERNAL_LEAK_FORBIDDEN`

    7: """

    9: from __future__ import annotations
   10: 
   11: from enum import Enum
   12: from typing import Union
   13: 
   14: 
   15: class DataClassification(str, Enum):
   16:     PUBLIC_SYNTHETIC = "PUBLIC_SYNTHETIC"
   17:     CAN_REAL = "CAN_REAL"
   18:     PRIVATE = "PRIVATE"
   19:     CLIENT = "CLIENT"
   20:     UNKNOWN = "UNKNOWN"
   21: 
   22: 
   23: ALL_CLASSIFICATIONS: tuple[DataClassification, ...] = tuple(DataClassification)
   24: 
   25: EXTERNAL_LEAK_FORBIDDEN: frozenset[DataClassification] = frozenset(
   26:     {
   27:         DataClassification.CAN_REAL,
   28:         DataClassification.PRIVATE,
   29:         DataClassification.CLIENT,
   30:         DataClassification.UNKNOWN,
   31:     }
   32: )
   33: 
   34: 
   35: def parse_classification(
   36:     value: Union[str, DataClassification, None],
   37: ) -> DataClassification:
   38:     """Normalize input to DataClassification. None → UNKNOWN. Invalid → ValueError."""
   39:     if value is None:
   40:         return DataClassification.UNKNOWN
   41:     if isinstance(value, DataClassification):
   42:         return value
   43:     return DataClassification(value)
   44: 
   45: 
   46: def is_external_leak_forbidden(classification: DataClassification) -> bool:
   47:     """True iff the given classification is forbidden from external-API egress."""
   48:     return classification in EXTERNAL_LEAK_FORBIDDEN

  155: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  156: # BUG-B-101 fix: unified manifest.status taxonomy.
  157: #
  158: # Pre-fix, successful runs wrote manifest.json WITHOUT a "status" key
  159: # while abort runs DID include it. Documentation claimed
  160: # manifest.status was authoritative — it wasn't. See
  161: # outputs/codex_findings/deep_dive_round_1/findings.md for the full
  162: # scoping analysis.
  163: #
  164: # Post-fix, EVERY exit path writes a manifest.json with a "status"
  165: # field from this unified taxonomy. `summary["status"]` is preserved
  166: # as secondary sweep telemetry for backward compatibility with any
  167: # downstream counter that relied on the legacy labels.
  168: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  169: 
  170: UNIFIED_STATUS_VALUES: frozenset[str] = frozenset({
  171:     # success
  172:     "success",
  173:     # partial — report produced but degraded signal
  174:     "partial_thin_corpus",
  175:     "partial_incomplete_corpus",
  176:     "partial_rule_check_warnings",
  177:     "partial_outline_fallback",      # BUG-M-203: planner failed, fallback used
  178:     "partial_qwen_advisory",         # BUG-M-205: Qwen judge flagged critical axes
  179:     # abort — pipeline refused to produce a report
  180:     "abort_scope_rejected",
  181:     "abort_no_sources",
  182:     "abort_corpus_inadequate",
  183:     "abort_corpus_approval_denied",
  184:     "abort_no_verified_sections",
  185:     "abort_evaluator_critical",      # BUG-M-205: PT08/PT11/PT12 integrity failure
  186:     # error — unhandled exception
  187:     "error_unexpected",
  188: })
  189: 
  190: # Map legacy summary["status"] labels → unified manifest.status values.
  191: _SUMMARY_TO_UNIFIED: dict[str, str] = {
  192:     "ok": "success",
  193:     "ok_thin_corpus": "partial_thin_corpus",
  194:     "ok_incomplete_corpus": "partial_incomplete_corpus",
  195:     "ok_outline_fallback": "partial_outline_fallback",
  196:     "ok_qwen_advisory": "partial_qwen_advisory",
  197:     "warn_rule_checks": "partial_rule_check_warnings",
  198:     "fail_no_sources": "abort_no_sources",
  199:     "fail_no_verified_prose": "abort_no_verified_sections",
  200:     "abort_scope_rejected": "abort_scope_rejected",
  201:     "abort_corpus_inadequate": "abort_corpus_inadequate",
  202:     "abort_corpus_approval_denied": "abort_corpus_approval_denied",
  203:     "abort_no_verified_sections": "abort_no_verified_sections",
  204:     "abort_evaluator_critical": "abort_evaluator_critical",
  205:     "error": "error_unexpected",
  206: }
  207: 
  208: 
  209: def to_unified_status(summary_status: str) -> str:
  210:     """Map a legacy summary["status"] label to the unified
  211:     manifest.status taxonomy. Unknown labels become error_unexpected
  212:     (fail loudly for the reader; still a valid taxonomy value)."""
  213:     return _SUMMARY_TO_UNIFIED.get(summary_status, "error_unexpected")
  214: 
  215: 
  216: def expected_str_for_abort(protocol: dict) -> str:
  217:     """Render expected tier distribution for abort-artifact text."""
  218:     parts = []
  219:     for entry in protocol.get("expected_tier_distribution", []) or []:
  220:         tier = entry.get("tier")
  221:         mn = (entry.get("min_fraction", 0) or 0) * 100
  222:         mx = (entry.get("max_fraction", 1) or 1) * 100
  223:         if tier:
  224:             parts.append(f"{tier} {mn:.0f}-{mx:.0f}%")
  225:     return ", ".join(parts) or "per scope template"
  226: 
  227: 
  228: def _base_manifest_envelope(
  229:     *,
  230:     run_id: str,
  231:     q: dict,
  232:     retrieval=None,
  233:     run_cost: float = 0.0,
  234: ) -> dict:
  235:     """BUG-SCHEMA-R8d fix: every manifest (success AND abort) carries
  236:     the same envelope so downstream consumers get consistent keys
  237:     regardless of exit path.
  238: 
  239:     Caller adds status-specific fields on top (adequacy, generator,
  240:     evaluator_gate, scope, error, etc.). Using this helper prevents
  241:     the envelope from drifting between exit paths.
  242:     """
  243:     env: dict = {
  244:         "run_id": run_id,
  245:         "slug": q.get("slug", ""),
  246:         "domain": q.get("domain", ""),

  228: def _base_manifest_envelope(
  229:     *,
  230:     run_id: str,
  231:     q: dict,
  232:     retrieval=None,
  233:     run_cost: float = 0.0,
  234: ) -> dict:
  235:     """BUG-SCHEMA-R8d fix: every manifest (success AND abort) carries
  236:     the same envelope so downstream consumers get consistent keys
  237:     regardless of exit path.
  238: 
  239:     Caller adds status-specific fields on top (adequacy, generator,
  240:     evaluator_gate, scope, error, etc.). Using this helper prevents
  241:     the envelope from drifting between exit paths.
  242:     """
  243:     env: dict = {
  244:         "run_id": run_id,
  245:         "slug": q.get("slug", ""),
  246:         "domain": q.get("domain", ""),
  247:         "question": q.get("question", ""),
  248:         "cost_usd": run_cost,
  249:         "budget_cap_usd": PG_MAX_COST_PER_RUN,
  250:     }
  251:     if retrieval is not None:
  252:         env["retrieval"] = {
  253:             "pre_filter": getattr(retrieval, "total_candidates_pre_filter", 0),
  254:             "fetched": getattr(retrieval, "candidates_fetched", 0),
  255:             "failed": getattr(retrieval, "candidates_failed_fetch", 0),
  256:             "api_calls": getattr(retrieval, "api_calls", {}),
  257:         }
  258:     return env

  260: 
  261: def write_per_run_cost_ledger(run_dir: Path, run_id: str) -> int:
  262:     """BUG-M-206 fix (deep-dive R8): filter the global cost ledger for
  263:     entries tagged with this run_id and write a per-run copy to
  264:     <run_dir>/cost_ledger.jsonl. Returns the count of entries written.
  265: 
  266:     The global ledger stays authoritative (monotonic append-only log),
  267:     but per-run consumers don't have to grep it by run_id anymore.
  268:     """
  269:     global_path = Path(
  270:         os.environ.get("PG_COST_LEDGER_PATH", "logs/pg_cost_ledger.jsonl")
  271:     )
  272:     if not global_path.exists():
  273:         return 0
  274:     out_path = run_dir / "cost_ledger.jsonl"
  275:     n = 0
  276:     try:
  277:         with open(global_path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as src, \
  278:                 open(out_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as dst:
  279:             for line in src:
  280:                 line = line.rstrip("\n")
  281:                 if not line:
  282:                     continue
  283:                 try:
  284:                     entry = json.loads(line)
  285:                 except json.JSONDecodeError:
  286:                     continue
  287:                 if entry.get("session_id") == run_id:
  288:                     dst.write(line + "\n")
  289:                     n += 1
  290:     except OSError as exc:
  291:         logging.getLogger(__name__).warning(
  292:             "per-run cost ledger write failed: %s", exc,
  293:         )
  294:     return n
  295: 
  296: 
  297: def filter_verified_sections(sections) -> list:
  298:     """Codex round 1 B-3: the single-source-of-truth predicate for
  299:     "did this section survive Phase-4 strict_verify?". A section
  300:     qualifies only if it was NOT dropped AND has non-empty verified_text.
  301:     """
  302:     return [
  303:         sr for sr in sections
  304:         if not getattr(sr, "dropped_due_to_failure", True)
  305:         and getattr(sr, "verified_text", "")
  306:     ]

    1: """I-arch-001a — single helper for v6-mode manifest augmentation.
    2: 
    3: Pipeline-A writes manifest.json at 6 sites (line refs in run_honest_sweep_r3.py:
    4: 1331/1453/1667/1746/2303/2806). When v6_mode is active, each call routes
    5: through augment_v6_manifest() to add the v6 fields the API + run_store +
    6: F-snowball bridge require. When v6_mode is False, manifest stays byte-
    7: identical to today (no key added).
    8: """
    9: 
   10: from __future__ import annotations
   11: 
   12: from typing import Any
   13: 
   14: 
   15: def augment_v6_manifest(
   16:     manifest: dict[str, Any],
   17:     *,
   18:     external_run_id: str | None,
   19:     decision_id: str | None,
   20:     query_slug: str | None,
   21:     retrieval_block: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
   22:     adequacy_block: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
   23:     models_block: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
   24: ) -> dict[str, Any]:
   25:     """Return augmented manifest dict. Does not mutate input.
   26: 
   27:     Non-v6 invocations (external_run_id is None) get the input back
   28:     unchanged — pipeline-A's existing behavior is preserved byte-for-byte.
   29:     """
   30:     if external_run_id is None:
   31:         return manifest
   32: 
   33:     augmented = dict(manifest)
   34:     augmented["external_run_id"] = external_run_id
   35:     augmented["query_slug"] = query_slug
   36: 
   37:     scope = dict(augmented.get("scope") or {})
   38:     scope["decision_id"] = decision_id
   39:     augmented["scope"] = scope
   40: 
   41:     if retrieval_block is not None:
   42:         augmented["retrieval"] = retrieval_block
   43:     if adequacy_block is not None:
   44:         augmented["adequacy"] = adequacy_block
   45:     if models_block is not None:
   46:         augmented["models"] = models_block
   47: 
   48:     return augmented

 2200: def _merge_bibliographies(
 2201:     section_slices: list[list[dict[str, Any]]],
 2202: ) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
 2203:     """Merge per-section biblios into a single ordered bibliography,
 2204:     remapping section-local citation numbers to global numbers."""
 2205:     # Each section's biblio has its own 1-based numbering. We need to
 2206:     # renumber globally, but the section's verified_text already has
 2207:     # [1][2][3] markers in section-local space.
 2208:     # Simpler approach: return the raw per-section biblios flattened,
 2209:     # deduped by evidence_id, and let the caller remap the inline
 2210:     # markers in a separate pass.
 2211:     seen: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}

 2226: def _remap_section_markers_to_global(
 2227:     section_results: list[SectionResult],
 2228:     global_biblio: list[dict[str, Any]],
 2229: ) -> list[str]:
 2230:     """Rewrite each section's [N] markers from section-local to global.
 2231: 
 2232:     Returns a list of remapped section prose strings.
 2233:     """
 2234:     ev_to_global = {b["evidence_id"]: b["num"] for b in global_biblio}
 2235:     remapped: list[str] = []
 2236:     for sect in section_results:
 2237:         if not sect.verified_text:
 2238:             continue
 2239:         # Build a mapping section-local-num -> global-num
 2240:         local_to_global: dict[int, int] = {}
 2241:         for entry in sect.biblio_slice:
 2242:             local_num = entry.get("num")
 2243:             ev_id = entry.get("evidence_id", "")
 2244:             global_num = ev_to_global.get(ev_id)
 2245:             if local_num is not None and global_num is not None:
 2246:                 local_to_global[local_num] = global_num
 2247:         text = sect.verified_text
 2248: 
 2249:         # Replace [N] markers using the mapping. Do the replace with a
 2250:         # callable to avoid subsequent substitutions clobbering each
 2251:         # other (e.g., [1] -> [5] -> [15]).
 2252:         def _replace(match: re.Match) -> str:
 2253:             n = int(match.group(1))
 2254:             g = local_to_global.get(n)
 2255:             return f"[{g}]" if g else match.group(0)

src/polaris_graph\generator\multi_section_generator.py:237:- **M-40: Mechanism section is the narrative-depth lever.** When AT LEAST 3 evidence rows in the summary above contain mechanism-of-action vocabulary — in either the `title:` field or the statement body — you MUST include "Mechanism" as one of the outline sections (5 by default, 6 when regulatory evidence is also present per M-41a above). Trigger vocabulary (any of, case-insensitive): "mechanism", "pharmacokinetic", "pharmacodynamic", "receptor", "half-life", "bioavailability", "metabolism", "agonist", "antagonist", "binding", "signaling", "pathway", "kinetic". A research-grade synthesis explains WHY the intervention works, not only WHETHER it works. Top-tier Deep Research outputs (GPT-5.4 DR, Gemini 3.1 Pro DR) dedicate a full section to mechanism/pharmacology for any clinical efficacy question; a report without it reads as a short brief rather than a deep synthesis. This rule is generalizable: in materials/chemistry a Mechanism section covers reaction pathway / phase transition / interface chemistry; in policy it covers causal pathway / incentive mechanism / enforcement mechanism; in finance it covers transmission channel / market microstructure.

  305: def wrap_evidence_for_prompt(
  306:     evidence_id: str,
  307:     statement: str,
  308:     direct_quote: str,
  309:     source_url: str = "",
  310:     tier: str = "",
  311: ) -> str:
  312:     """Wrap evidence in the delimited form the generator expects.
  313: 
  314:     Uses fixed delimiters `<<<evidence:...>>>` and `<<<end_evidence>>>`.
  315:     These are deliberately not standard XML so that a bad actor who
  316:     tries to spoof closing tags can't trivially break out.
  317:     """
  318:     statement_s, r1 = sanitize_evidence_text(statement)
  319:     quote_s, r2 = sanitize_evidence_text(direct_quote)
  320:     total_red = r1 + r2
  321:     if total_red > 0:
  322:         logger.warning(
  323:             "[provenance_generator] Redacted %d prompt-injection pattern(s) "
  324:             "from evidence %s",
  325:             total_red, evidence_id,
  326:         )
  327:     return (
  328:         f"<<<evidence:{evidence_id}>>>\n"
  329:         f"tier: {tier}\n"
  330:         f"url: {source_url}\n"
  331:         f"statement: {statement_s}\n"
  332:         f"direct_quote: {quote_s}\n"
  333:         f"<<<end_evidence>>>"
  334:     )
  335: 
  336: 
  337: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  338: # Provenance token parsing
  339: # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  340: 
  341: # Pattern: [#ev:<evidence_id>:<start>-<end>]
  342: # Example: [#ev:ev_step1:12-45]
  343: _PROVENANCE_TOKEN_RE = re.compile(
  344:     r"\[#ev:(?P<ev_id>[A-Za-z0-9_]+):(?P<start>\d+)-(?P<end>\d+)\]"
  345: )
  346: 
  347: 
  348: @dataclass
  349: class ProvenanceToken:
  350:     evidence_id: str
  351:     start: int
  352:     end: int
  353:     raw: str
  354: 
  355:     @property
  356:     def span_len(self) -> int:
  357:         return self.end - self.start
  358: 
  359: 
  360: @dataclass
  361: class SentenceVerification:
  362:     sentence: str
  363:     tokens: list[ProvenanceToken]

  366:     resolved_citation_marker: str = ""   # e.g., "[1]"
  367:     # Gap-2: soft warnings that don't trigger a drop but get surfaced
  368:     # to the evaluator (stored as PT13 in external_evaluator).
  369:     soft_warnings: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)

 1026: def resolve_provenance_to_citations(
 1027:     kept_sentences: list[SentenceVerification],
 1028:     evidence_pool: dict[str, dict[str, Any]],
 1029: ) -> tuple[str, list[dict[str, Any]]]:
 1030:     """Strip [#ev:...] tokens and replace with numbered citations.
 1031: 
 1032:     Returns (rendered_text, bibliography_list). Bibliography is a list
 1033:     of dicts: {num, evidence_id, url, tier, statement}.
 1034:     """
 1035:     ev_to_num: dict[str, int] = {}
 1036:     biblio: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
 1037: 
 1038:     def _num_for(ev_id: str) -> int:
 1039:         if ev_id not in ev_to_num:
 1040:             ev_to_num[ev_id] = len(ev_to_num) + 1
 1041:             ev = evidence_pool.get(ev_id, {})
 1042:             biblio.append({
 1043:                 "num": ev_to_num[ev_id],
 1044:                 "evidence_id": ev_id,
 1045:                 "url": ev.get("source_url", ""),
 1046:                 "tier": ev.get("tier", ""),
 1047:                 "statement": (ev.get("statement") or "")[:300],
 1048:             })
 1049:         return ev_to_num[ev_id]
 1050: 
 1051:     findings_lines: list[str] = []
 1052:     limitations_lines: list[str] = []
 1053:     for sv in kept_sentences:
 1054:         # Strip provenance tokens first so degenerate fragments can be
 1055:         # detected before we assign citation numbers (otherwise the
 1056:         # bibliography keeps an entry whose only citing sentence we
 1057:         # later drop).
 1058:         stripped = _PROVENANCE_TOKEN_RE.sub("", sv.sentence).strip()
 1059:         # Clean trailing spaces before punctuation
 1060:         stripped = re.sub(r"\s+([.!?,;])", r"\1", stripped)
 1061:         # BUG-M-8 (Codex pass 9): drop degenerate sentence fragments
 1062:         # that survive strict_verify as bare punctuation + citation
 1063:         # (observed in the Novo sweep as ".[4]", "Morgan analysts.[12]",
 1064:         # ".[14]" between legitimate sentences). A real sentence has
 1065:         # ≥3 content words AND ≥15 chars of prose after provenance
 1066:         # stripping. Lower bounds deliberately conservative — the
 1067:         # shortest legitimate research sentences in smoke runs
 1068:         # ("No contradictions detected.") comfortably clear it.
 1069:         _content_w = re.findall(r"[A-Za-z]+", stripped)
 1070:         if len(_content_w) < 3 or len(stripped) < 15:
 1071:             continue
 1072:         # Assign citation numbers only for surviving sentences
 1073:         used_nums: list[int] = []
 1074:         for tok in sv.tokens:
 1075:             n = _num_for(tok.evidence_id)
 1076:             if n not in used_nums:
 1077:                 used_nums.append(n)
 1078:         # Append citation markers
 1079:         markers = "".join(f"[{n}]" for n in used_nums)
 1080:         sentence_out = stripped + markers
 1081: 
 1082:         # Gap-3: put Limitations sentences in a separate paragraph so
 1083:         # they render on their own line in the final report.
 1084:         if any("limitations_paragraph_pass_through" in w for w in sv.soft_warnings):
 1085:             limitations_lines.append(sentence_out)

  610: 
  611:     Checks:
  612:       1. Evidence ID exists in pool.
  613:       2. Span bounds are within evidence direct_quote length.

  615:          each number must appear in the claimed span text.
  616:     """
  617:     tokens = parse_provenance_tokens(sentence)
  618:     failures: list[str] = []
  619: 
  620:     # Strip provenance tokens for numeric matching to avoid matching
  621:     # the span numbers themselves (e.g., [#ev:x:12-45] has 12 and 45).
  622:     sentence_for_numbers = _PROVENANCE_TOKEN_RE.sub(" ", sentence).strip()
  623: 
  624:     if not tokens:
  625:         # Sentences without provenance are rejected outright.

  635:     # from DIFFERENT cited spans — the ICER trial's 86.6% treatment

  639:     #
  640:     # Also: placebo-arm numbers (e.g., "vs 2.4% with placebo") and
  641:     # achievement thresholds ("≥5%") are filtered from the set of

  691:             for tok in tokens:
  692:                 ev = evidence_pool.get(tok.evidence_id)
  693:                 if ev is None:
  694:                     continue
  695:                 direct_quote = ev.get("direct_quote") or ev.get("statement") or ""
  696:                 span_text = direct_quote[tok.start:tok.end]

  698:             if sentence_numbers and not (sentence_numbers & aggregated_span_numbers):
  699:                 ev_ids = ",".join(sorted({t.evidence_id for t in tokens}))
  700:                 failures.append(

  702:                 )
  703: 
  704:         # Codex round 1 B-1: semantic grounding for non-numeric claims.
  705:         # A sentence like "Semaglutide improved sleep quality [#ev:ev1:0-20]"
  706:         # used to pass verification because it had no numbers — only the
  707:         # numeric-mismatch branches ran. Now we ALSO require at least
  708:         # MIN_CONTENT_WORD_OVERLAP content words (non-stopword, >=3 chars)
  709:         # to appear in the aggregated cited-span text. Zero overlap =
  710:         # unsupported claim, sentence dropped.
  711:         sentence_content = _content_words(sentence_stripped)
  712:         span_content = _content_words(" ".join(aggregated_span_text))
  713:         if sentence_content:
  714:             overlap = sentence_content & span_content
  715:             if len(overlap) < MIN_CONTENT_WORD_OVERLAP:
  716:                 ev_ids = ",".join(sorted({t.evidence_id for t in tokens}))
  717:                 failures.append(
  718:                     f"no_content_word_overlap_any_cited_span:{ev_ids}:"
  719:                     f"sentence_words={sorted(sentence_content)[:5]}"

   44: def _load_uploaded_documents(
   45:     document_ids: list[str], ingester: Any = None, chunk_size: int = 1500,
   46: ) -> list[dict]:
   47:     """Load chunks for given document_ids from DocumentIngester.
   48: 
   49:     Per I-f3-001. Validates each doc_id against 16-hex format (matches
   50:     `hashlib.sha256(file_bytes).hexdigest()[:16]` per document_ingester.py:162)
   51:     BEFORE filesystem lookup to prevent path traversal. Skips invalid /
   52:     missing IDs with a logged warning. Raises RuntimeError if every
   53:     requested ID failed (LAW II — fail loud).
   54:     """
   55:     if not document_ids:
   56:         return []
   57:     if ingester is None:
   58:         from src.polaris_graph.document_ingester import DocumentIngester
   59:         ingester = DocumentIngester()
   60:     out: list[dict] = []
   61:     for doc_id in document_ids:
   62:         if not _DOC_ID_RE.fullmatch(doc_id):
   63:             logger.warning("[v4 graph] invalid doc_id format: %r", doc_id)
   64:             continue
   65:         doc = ingester.get_document(doc_id)
   66:         if doc is None:
   67:             logger.warning("[v4 graph] doc_id %s not found", doc_id)
   68:             continue
   69:         content = doc.get("content", "")
   70:         if not content:
   71:             logger.warning("[v4 graph] doc_id %s has empty content", doc_id)
   72:             continue
   73:         meta = doc.get("metadata", {})
   74:         name = meta.get("original_filename") or meta.get("filename") or doc_id
   75:         chunks = [content[i : i + chunk_size] for i in range(0, len(content), chunk_size)]
   76:         for idx, chunk_text in enumerate(chunks):
   77:             out.append({
   78:                 "document_id": doc_id, "filename": name,
   79:                 "chunk_index": idx, "text": chunk_text,
   80:             })
   81:     if not out:
   82:         raise RuntimeError(
   83:             f"_load_uploaded_documents: every requested document_id "
   84:             f"({len(document_ids)} ids) failed to resolve"
   85:         )
   86:     return out

  112: def _infer_domain(application: str, query: str) -> str:
  113:     """Return a scope-template domain. Default to 'custom' for
  114:     free-form UI queries that don't hint at clinical/tech/policy/dd."""
  115:     a = (application or "").lower()
  116:     if a in _DOMAIN_HINTS:
  117:         return _DOMAIN_HINTS[a]
  118:     q = (query or "").lower()
  119:     for key, dom in _DOMAIN_HINTS.items():
  120:         if key in q:
  121:             return dom
  122:     return "custom"

  - "There is no persisted full chunk list in upload.py; UploadResponse has content plus chunk_preview only. Implementation should re-chunk record.content at /runs, not treat chunk_preview as complete."
  - "Resolve/validate document_ids before insert_run/enqueue so a missing or unusable upload does not leave a queued orphan run."
  - "Queued/unparsed pdf/docx uploads with no content should fail loud for #506, not silently produce zero upload evidence."
  - "Blocked-doc observability cannot ride set_pipeline_meta directly; carry metadata-only blocked/used counts into q/manifest/result_json, and never log document text."
  - "Option (a) needs an explicit embedded-content cap or chunk cap because md/txt uploads can be 50MB despite the brief calling message size bounded."
content_transport_ruling: "option-a-embed: correct for #506/demo scope because it works across API/worker process boundaries without adding a durable store. Keep the follow-up durable store separate. Prefer resolving and validating at /runs, and include only allowed content plus metadata-only blocked records if broker trust is uncertain."
scope_ruling: "single-pr-cap-exemption: the work is one coherent acceptance path from POST /runs to generator evidence and manifest proof. A two-PR carve is only warranted if choosing the durable upload store."
merger_ruling: "direct-dict-rows-ok: pipeline-A generator/evidence_pool consumes dict rows, and matching the existing contract-row prepend is the lowest-risk path. Retrofitting evidence_pool_merger is separate hygiene."
